# Excalidraw Data

## Text Elements
if the function is concave up, the first derivative is constantly growing and therefore
the second derivative is positive ^yc51FFev

a matrix multiplied by itself, it has to be square ^4RG5xSNN

the matrix for which if you multiply the current matrix you get the identity
matrix back ^RGTuovwm

closed form is a form that express the nth term as a function of n ^M8Rwq4ez

define a sequence where each term is expressed as a function of the 
previous one ^ob8FId6y

a sequence where each term is obtained by adding a fixed number to the previous
or adding to the initial term this constant n times ^9uv3sGLN

the constant added to each term of an arithmetic sequence ^g9cm2KI0

a sequence where each term is obtained by multiplying the previus for a constant
or by multiplying for that constant n times in the case of a closed form ^yzgJFejG

C just scale each function ^ib8lyFX6

the sum of the members of a sequence ^d7tIVZ3F

if it is bounded the sum is the number it converges to ^jUHodaH8
